(****************************************************************

 In this file, we combine the facts from `precomp_ess_surj.v`
 and `precomp_fully_faithful.v`. We show that if we have a fully
 faithful and essential surjective functor `F : C‚ÇÅ ‚ü∂ C‚ÇÇ` and a
 univalent category `D`, then we have an adjoint equivalence
 between `[ C‚ÇÇ , D ]` and `[ C‚ÇÅ , D ]` (the functor is given
 by precomposition). We also give some functions to use this
 adjoint equivalence.

 ****************************************************************)

Section PrecompEquivalence.
  Context {C‚ÇÅ C‚ÇÇ : category}
          (D : univalent_category)
          (F : C‚ÇÅ ‚ü∂ C‚ÇÇ)
          (HF‚ÇÅ : essentially_surjective F)
          (HF‚ÇÇ : fully_faithful F).

adj_equivalence_of_cats
  (pre_composition_functor C‚ÇÅ C‚ÇÇ (pr1 D) F)

C‚ÇÅ, C‚ÇÇ: category

fully_faithful
  (pre_composition_functor C‚ÇÅ C‚ÇÇ (pr1 D) F)
 exact (pre_composition_with_ess_surj_and_fully_faithful_is_fully_faithful
               C‚ÇÅ C‚ÇÇ D
               F
               HF‚ÇÅ HF‚ÇÇ).
    
C‚ÇÅ, C‚ÇÇ: category
D: univalent_category
F: C‚ÇÅ ‚ü∂ C‚ÇÇ
HF‚ÇÅ: essentially_surjective F
HF‚ÇÇ: fully_faithful F
essentially_surjective
  (pre_composition_functor C‚ÇÅ C‚ÇÇ (pr1 D) F)
 exact (pre_composition_essentially_surjective
               C‚ÇÅ C‚ÇÇ D (pr2 D)
               F
               HF‚ÇÅ HF‚ÇÇ).
  Defined.

  Let L : [ C‚ÇÇ , D ] ‚ü∂ [ C‚ÇÅ , D ]
    := pre_composition_functor C‚ÇÅ C‚ÇÇ (pr1 D) F.
  Let R : [ C‚ÇÅ , D ] ‚ü∂ [ C‚ÇÇ , D ]
    := right_adjoint precomp_adjoint_equivalence.
  Let Œµ : nat_z_iso (R ‚àô L) (functor_identity _)
    := counit_nat_z_iso_from_adj_equivalence_of_cats
         precomp_adjoint_equivalence.
  Let Œ∑ : nat_z_iso (functor_identity _) (L ‚àô R)
    := unit_nat_z_iso_from_adj_equivalence_of_cats
         precomp_adjoint_equivalence.

  Definition lift_functor_along
             (G : C‚ÇÅ ‚ü∂ D)
    : C‚ÇÇ ‚ü∂ D
    := R G.

  Definition lift_functor_along_comm
             (G : C‚ÇÅ ‚ü∂ D)
    : nat_z_iso (F ‚àô lift_functor_along G) G
    := nat_z_iso_from_z_iso _ (nat_z_iso_pointwise_z_iso Œµ G).

  
C‚ÇÅ, C‚ÇÇ: category
D: univalent_category
F: C‚ÇÅ ‚ü∂ C‚ÇÇ
HF‚ÇÅ: essentially_surjective F
HF‚ÇÇ: fully_faithful F
L:= pre_composition_functor C‚ÇÅ C‚ÇÇ (pr1 D) F: [C‚ÇÇ, D] ‚ü∂ [C‚ÇÅ, D]
R:= right_adjoint precomp_adjoint_equivalence: [C‚ÇÅ, D] ‚ü∂ [C‚ÇÇ, D]
Œµ:= counit_nat_z_iso_from_adj_equivalence_of_cats
  precomp_adjoint_equivalence: nat_z_iso (R ‚àô L) (functor_identity [C‚ÇÅ, D])
Œ∑:= unit_nat_z_iso_from_adj_equivalence_of_cats
  precomp_adjoint_equivalence: nat_z_iso (functor_identity [C‚ÇÇ, D]) (L ‚àô R)
G‚ÇÅ, G‚ÇÇ: C‚ÇÇ ‚ü∂ D
Œ±: F ‚àô G‚ÇÅ ‚üπ F ‚àô G‚ÇÇ
G‚ÇÅ ‚üπ G‚ÇÇ

  
C‚ÇÅ, C‚ÇÇ: category
D: univalent_category
F: C‚ÇÅ ‚ü∂ C‚ÇÇ
HF‚ÇÅ: essentially_surjective F
HF‚ÇÇ: fully_faithful F
L:= pre_composition_functor C‚ÇÅ C‚ÇÇ (pr1 D) F: [C‚ÇÇ, D] ‚ü∂ [C‚ÇÅ, D]
R:= right_adjoint precomp_adjoint_equivalence: [C‚ÇÅ, D] ‚ü∂ [C‚ÇÇ, D]
Œµ:= counit_nat_z_iso_from_adj_equivalence_of_cats
  precomp_adjoint_equivalence: nat_z_iso (R ‚àô L) (functor_identity [C‚ÇÅ, D])
Œ∑:= unit_nat_z_iso_from_adj_equivalence_of_cats
  precomp_adjoint_equivalence: nat_z_iso (functor_identity [C‚ÇÇ, D]) (L ‚àô R)
G‚ÇÅ, G‚ÇÇ: C‚ÇÇ ‚ü∂ D
Œ±: F ‚àô G‚ÇÅ ‚üπ F ‚àô G‚ÇÇ
G‚ÇÅ ‚üπ G‚ÇÇ

    exact (invmap
             (make_weq
                _
                (fully_faithful_from_equivalence
                   _ _ _
                   precomp_adjoint_equivalence
                   G‚ÇÅ G‚ÇÇ))
          Œ±).
  Defined.

Œ±: F ‚àô G‚ÇÅ ‚üπ F ‚àô G‚ÇÇ
pre_whisker F (lift_nat_trans_along Œ±) = Œ±

D: univalent_category

    exact (homotweqinvweq
             (make_weq
                _
                (fully_faithful_from_equivalence
                   _ _ _
                   precomp_adjoint_equivalence
                   G‚ÇÅ G‚ÇÇ))
             Œ±).
  Qed.

    exact (maponpaths
             pr1
             (proofirrelevance
                _
                (pr2 (fully_faithful_implies_full_and_faithful
                        _ _ _
                        (fully_faithful_from_equivalence
                           _ _ _
                           precomp_adjoint_equivalence))
                   G‚ÇÅ G‚ÇÇ
                   (pre_whisker F Œ≤‚ÇÇ))
                (Œ≤‚ÇÅ ,, p)
                (Œ≤‚ÇÇ ,, idpath _))).
  Qed.

Œ∑:= unit_nat_z_iso_from_adj_equivalence_of_cats
  precomp_adjoint_equivalence: nat_z_iso (functor_identity [C‚ÇÇ, D]) (L ‚àô R)
G‚ÇÅ, G‚ÇÇ: C‚ÇÇ ‚ü∂ D
Œ±: nat_z_iso (F ‚àô G‚ÇÅ) (F ‚àô G‚ÇÇ)
Œ≤:= z_iso_from_nat_z_iso D Œ±: z_iso (F ‚àô G‚ÇÅ) (F ‚àô G‚ÇÇ)
is_z_isomorphism (lift_nat_trans_along Œ±)

    
C‚ÇÅ, C‚ÇÇ: category
D: univalent_category
F: C‚ÇÅ ‚ü∂ C‚ÇÇ
HF‚ÇÅ: essentially_surjective F
HF‚ÇÇ: fully_faithful F
L:= pre_composition_functor C‚ÇÅ C‚ÇÇ (pr1 D) F: [C‚ÇÇ, D] ‚ü∂ [C‚ÇÅ, D]
R:= right_adjoint precomp_adjoint_equivalence: [C‚ÇÅ, D] ‚ü∂ [C‚ÇÇ, D]
Œµ:= counit_nat_z_iso_from_adj_equivalence_of_cats
  precomp_adjoint_equivalence: nat_z_iso (R ‚àô L) (functor_identity [C‚ÇÅ, D])
Œ∑:= unit_nat_z_iso_from_adj_equivalence_of_cats
  precomp_adjoint_equivalence: nat_z_iso (functor_identity [C‚ÇÇ, D]) (L ‚àô R)
G‚ÇÅ, G‚ÇÇ: C‚ÇÇ ‚ü∂ D
Œ±: nat_z_iso (F ‚àô G‚ÇÅ) (F ‚àô G‚ÇÇ)
Œ≤:= z_iso_from_nat_z_iso D Œ±: z_iso (F ‚àô G‚ÇÅ) (F ‚àô G‚ÇÇ)
ff_precomp:= fully_faithful_from_equivalence
  [C‚ÇÇ, pr1 D] [C‚ÇÅ, pr1 D]
  (pre_composition_functor C‚ÇÅ C‚ÇÇ (pr1 D) F)
  precomp_adjoint_equivalence: fully_faithful
  (pre_composition_functor C‚ÇÅ C‚ÇÇ 
     (pr1 D) F)
is_z_isomorphism (lift_nat_trans_along Œ±)


    exact (fully_faithful_reflects_iso_proof
             [C‚ÇÇ, pr1 D] [C‚ÇÅ, pr1 D]
             (pre_composition_functor _ _ D F)
             ff_precomp _ _ Œ≤
          ).
  Defined.

End PrecompEquivalence.

    apply (pr2 q).
  Qed.

     (Œª x : C, identity ((functor_identity C ‚àô F) x))
     (lift_functor_along_id_subproof C D F) c)

      
C: category
D: univalent_category
F: C ‚ü∂ D
F_eso: essentially_surjective F
F_ff: fully_faithful F
c: C
is_inverse_in_precat
  (make_nat_trans (functor_identity C ‚àô F)
     (F ‚àô functor_identity D)
     (Œª x : C, identity ((functor_identity C ‚àô F) x))
     (lift_functor_along_id_subproof C D F) c)
  (identity ((F ‚àô functor_identity D) c))

      abstract (split ; apply id_right).
  Defined.

End LiftedFunctorsIdentity.

Section LiftedFunctorsPairFunctor.

  
C1, C2, D1, D2, E1, E2: category
F1: C1 ‚ü∂ D1
F2: D1 ‚ü∂ E1
G1: C2 ‚ü∂ D2
G2: D2 ‚ü∂ E2
nat_z_iso (pair_functor (F1 ‚àô F2) (G1 ‚àô G2))
  (pair_functor F1 G1 ‚àô pair_functor F2 G2)

  
C1, C2, D1, D2, E1, E2: category
F1: C1 ‚ü∂ D1
F2: D1 ‚ü∂ E1
G1: C2 ‚ü∂ D2
G2: D2 ‚ü∂ E2
nat_z_iso (pair_functor (F1 ‚àô F2) (G1 ‚àô G2))
  (pair_functor F1 G1 ‚àô pair_functor F2 G2)

    
C1, C2, D1, D2, E1, E2: category
F1: C1 ‚ü∂ D1
F2: D1 ‚ü∂ E1
G1: C2 ‚ü∂ D2
G2: D2 ‚ü∂ E2
pair_functor (F1 ‚àô F2) (G1 ‚àô G2)
‚üπ pair_functor F1 G1 ‚àô pair_functor F2 G2
C1, C2, D1, D2, E1, E2: category
F1: C1 ‚ü∂ D1
F2: D1 ‚ü∂ E1
G1: C2 ‚ü∂ D2

  Let FF' := pair_functor F1' F2'.

  Let FF_ff := pair_functor_ff _ _ F1_ff F2_ff.

‚ü∂ category_binproduct D1' D2'
